I have had several groomers for all my dogs over the years but this place is one in a million. A month ago my wife brought one of our Australian Shepherds in to get her shaved. She said the lady made her feel guilty about shaving an Aussie so she just had her groomed. The lady told her it was bad for their skin. The problem is, after winter she sheds an insane amount of hair. But...we tried what the groomer instructed and brushed her daily. She still shed so much, we only let her in at night. Our dogs live with us so this does not work. A month later I brought the same dog back to get shaved. My wife was so intimidated by this lady she did not want to take her. So I did. I thought my wife was exaggerating with the guilt experience. NEVER, NEVER, NEVER, in a thousand years did I ever think I'd be writing a review about a crazy groomer who is off her rocker, but her it is. She was overbearing,  rude, impossible to communicate with, and an absolute nightmare. The poor desk lady just sat there and listened in disbelief. After the groomer walked out, the desk lady apologized over and over again. My point is this! I would not recommend this place for ANY reason. If the groomer reads this, I know what she'd say. I (crazily) am just trying to protect the dogs. A. We tried your method, it did not work. B. BEING OUTSIDE ALL THE TIME, can't be better for the dog and not better for our family. C. We have owned NUMEROUS Aussies and have never had skin issues no matter what their age was. D. IT'S NOT YOUR DOG!!! Trying another groomer today. My wife was never more right about "The Crazy Groomer".</Text>

< review>
This is a fairly large smoke shop. They sell herbal supplements, vape items, cigars, smoking pipes and water pipes. You can get s small smoking pipe for $10 or spend $100+ on a Hookah. They also have cigarettes but you should quit those. They sell glass pieces made by local artist. I found a small glass spoon pipe made by someone in my home town for $30. Plus it glows in the dark!

Small children are allowed in on a case by case basis. This shop does require you to be at least 18 years old, and 21+ to buy most of items. So leave the kids at home.

Mask is required for entry.<//review>

<Time>1449282197294< /Time><Rating>4</Rating><review>Most non chain coffee shops are small by nature and such is the case here, but something that will probably give you pause and stop your order in it's tracks is the food menu. It's the largest coffee shop food menu I've seen with a few dozen breakfast and lunch sandwich's. I don't drink that much coffee as I try and stay away from caffeine, but it's a great regroup point for my longer rides from Oceanside.

Dog Friendly.

Probably some of the best service for a coffee shop around. While enjoying the patio someone will come out and ask if you need anything else, refills, napkins, etc. That's waiter service and at a coffee shop. To me the size and set up limit if from getting 5 starts, but the menu, price and service put it well above most places which are all about convenience.

Inside can get crowded and be a bit chaotic. They have excellent iced coffees. With Juice Nation nearby taking care of the juice crowd they here have focused more on the smoothie side of things because most juicers put aside the flavor for the benefits, not the case for the overly caffeinated.

Red, White bagel is classic even if overly priced, I go with the deluxe with the turkey, it's less breakfast that way. Tuna melt to me is quite good despite many people hating tuna, their mayo is subtle. It's not a sandwich shop, but it's quite a menu for a coffee shop. They do catering. Parking can suck despite being the center attraction, the other business tend to lock up the spaces spcificly adjacent to them.

Free Wifi and maybe it's me, but the lot always seems to be in, well paved condition.<//review>< pictures>

< Text>
Working with Lang Antique & Estate Jewelry was an easy and wonderful experience.  I had heard about them through a referral who told me that they had engagement diamond rings in the price range that I was looking for and in the style I desired the most.

I didn't know what to expect but when going through the website, there were pieces I found myself very interested in!   However, I live in MA and they are in San Francisco so I assumed the process would be way too difficult and I wouldn't be able to work with them.  That was, until I called them...

Nicole Corsini made purchasing my engagement ring easy, fun and stress free.   Because I live far away, she explained and made me feel comfortable about shipping rings across the coast and how easy the return was if I didn't like the piece.   She also explained I could do it as many times as I wanted and have even a few rings shipped to me at once to decide from.

After telling her which rings I liked from the website, she immediately took clearer photos and videos of them to give me a better sense of what they looked like!  It was easier to narrow down which ring I liked the best!  Her photos were as if I was in the room trying them on.   Then they shipped the ring!

After trying on only one ring, I fell in love and was sold!

Lang Antiques was very professional from the beginning.   Made the process of making an important decision very easy having been no where near them.   When they shipped the ring to me after it was resized (FOR FREE), it was during a very bad snowstorm.  There was someone from the company who emailed me about the delay of the delivery, clearly tracking the package with me too!  I was very impressed by that.

Lang also offers a layaway program which was very helpful to me and my new fiance!   We were given a few months to pay it off instead of doing it all in one shot.    I felt safe throughout the entire process.   I highly recommend working with them even if you live nowhere near San Franciso.  The distance didn't matter.    Nicole was amazing and I am truly grateful!

- Shira Wilkofsky</Text>

<Rating>5<//Rating><Review>Lang has an amazing selection of vintage and antique jewelry accompanied by exceptional customer service!

I had been eyeing this store through their Instagram site for a while, and when my fiance and I went in to browse for engagement rings they did not disappoint. They have an amazing selection that is well curated and organized, and they get in new stock frequently. They do have very high end jewelry, but also many quite affordable rings in a good range for every budget.

Our sales associate, Molly, was knowledgeable, friendly, patient, and fun. She indulged me as I tried on many, many rings (and a few bracelets and necklaces...), and I never felt like she was trying to rush me in a decision, but at the same time she was really helpful in helping us narrow down our choices and figure out which rings we liked best. I am very indecisive and didn't go into the process knowing exactly which style I wanted, and Molly was also really good at quickly figuring out my taste and suggesting options I was likely to enjoy. We were definitely looking at items in the lowest price range of their selection, but I never felt like we were treated as such. At the end, I was deciding between two rings, and one was almost double the price of the other, but I never felt like I was being nudged to purchase the more expensive one. We ended up with a gorgeous ring that I am so happy with, and we also learned that engagement ring purchases get you a 10% discount on wedding bands.

They are unusual compared to many other antique jewelers in SF in that you can just walk in anytime. We went in on a Tuesday afternoon and had the store almost to ourselves. When we went back on a Thursday it was more crowded, so I might recommend going on an earlier weekday.

We had a great experience at Lang with Molly and the rest of the staff, and I would recommend this place to anyone who wants some unique and beautiful jewelry!!<//Review>< Pics>

<name>Mickey Scherrer<//name><date>1504458817529</date><Rate>5</Rate>< Review>
I purchased an engagement ring for my girlfriend in July 2017 online from Lang Antiques. I was looking for something vintage and unique and didn't want to deal with the Diamond District. I came across Lang's website and almost immediately found a ring that I thought would be perfect. I browsed around other shops, but kept coming back to Lang as their information on the ring was thorough and their prices seemed very reasonable. They also have a great return and resizing policy, so I didn't have to worry about getting stuck with a less than perfect ring.

I was hesitant to make such a large purchase online, so I reached out to Lang to inquire more about the ring and resizing. Nicole got back to me right away with more information and even offered to send more photographs of the ring. Even better news, she let me know they were having a Summer Sale on their jewelry. She helped me set up shipping to my Ma's house upstate (no doorman!) and contacted me at each step of the shipping and resizing process. Their website said that resizing can take up to two weeks, but they seemed to have done it overnight!

I proposed during the eclipse in Central Park and my soon to be wife absolutely loved the ring! Nicole followed up with me soon after to see how everything went and if we needed any additional size adjustments. Awesome customer service and a great shop! I highly recommend working with Lang if you are looking for something unique.<//Review>

< review>
I encourage locals and out-of-towners to stop in to Lang's, preferably on a weekday when the shop is not neck deep in customers.  No money? No problem. Lang Antiques offers beautiful items at all price points, and usually there are one-of-a-kind items. It is independently owned (i.e., not a piece of some huge corporate conglomerate) and consequently Lang's is all about customer satisfaction. The owner, Suzanne, enjoys high respect from her local and international colleagues, including the large auction houses. Lang's welcomes you to admire, converse with knowledgeable experts with deep insight into the historical significance of gems and objets d'art, and leave with more knowledge and deepened appreciation of wearable antiques as an art form, as living pieces of history, and of the craftsmanship behind what many regard as merely luxury items.

This atelier is beautifully appointed, easy to find, a feast for the eyes, and one of the long-term prides of San Francisco. Enjoy!<//review>

< Text>
My husband recently bought me a ring from Lang Antiques. This was for our anniversary and he told me to find the ring I wanted. I looked for weeks because I had in my mind exactly what I wanted. We went to jewelers and shops . Becoming quite frustrated with the cookie-cutter look of every ring I saw, I decided to look online when I came across Lang Antiques and their website. I wanted something different, something original, something with a story, heritage... and I found it.  This ring is gorgeous and even now I look at it several times a day and think just how lucky I am that my husband bought it for me for our anniversary.

It sparkles and shines and is absolutely beautiful in any light.  What I love most about it is the history behind it, its age, and the fact that it looks completely different than any ring sold today.  It is my very favorite piece of jewelry and I am excited to one day pass it down to my children.

I talk about Lang Antiques to anyone who will listen.  The customer care was phenominal and all my questions were answered in such a timely manner.  Even when the ring went back after sizing to have diamonds reinforced, someone called me to tell me about the delay in shipping and then offered to overnight the ring to me. Spending a sizable amount of money on something sight unseen is a difficult thing but Nicole at Lang assured me and helped with any and every question I had along the way. The pictures posted are true and vivid. The staff is incredible.  All in all, it was a great experience.  Thank you, thank you, thank you for such a beautiful ring that is rich with heritage.  I am so pleased!

Christy May
Indiana<//Text>
